With an av. potential of 2.75 V vs. sodium metal, layered NaMn3O5 exhibits a high energy d. of 602 W-h/kg, and also presents good rate capability.  Furthermore, the diffusion coeff. of sodium ions in the layered NaMn3O5 electrode is investigated by using the galvanostatic intermittent titrn. technique.  The results greatly contribute to the development of room-temp. sodium-ion batteries based on earth-abundant elements.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGp1NzH8uNL8w7Vg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lg1G2EbOQyYZA"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2cXps1ynsLw%253D&amp;md5=09cb2baa413ef21fc899dced87e9c9e0</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref43"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref43" class="rightTabRefNumLink">43</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit43" data-doi="10.1146/annurev-matsci-070909-104435"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Tang, M.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Carter, W. C.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Chiang, Y.-M.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Electrochemically Driven Phase Transitions in Insertion Electrodes for Lithium-Ion Batteries: Examples in Lithium Metal Phosphate Olivines</span>. <i>Annu. Rev. Mater. Res.</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2010</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>40</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">501</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">529</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1146/annurev-matsci-070909-104435</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit43R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">43</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Electrochemically driven phase transitions in insertion electrodes for lithium-ion batteries: examples in lithium metal phosphate olivines</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Tang, Ming; Carter, W. Craig; Chiang, Yet-Ming</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Annual Review of Materials Research</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2010</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">40</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue"></span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">501-529</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">ARMRCU</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1531-7331</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Annual Reviews Inc.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">A review.  The thermodn. and kinetics of phase transformations in electrochem. systems are reviewed.  Phase transitions in LiMPO4 (M = Fe, Mn, Ni, Co) olivines are highlighted.  The phase transformation phenomena in LiMPO4 are diverse and include thermodn. effects of particle size and applied overpotential, the appearance of metastable phases, and the effects of defects from at. disorder and aliovalent doping.  Such phenomena also include kinetic effects such as interface motion and diffusion of Li-electron complexes.  The nature of phase transitions directly influences electrode performance in battery applications.  Reduced particle size and doping can reduce or eliminate room-temp. Li miscibility gaps, which in turn affect characteristics of state of charge vs. voltage and the elastic energy due to vol. mismatches between phases.  Near the conditions for a phase transition, Li diffusion coeffs. are reduced.  Nucleation and growth kinetics produce a series of phase transition sequences, which can result in the accumulation of noncryst. phases during electrochem. cycling.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGoxOB__opnJ67Vg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lg1G2EbOQyYZA"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC3cXhtVClt7bI&amp;md5=e578f53bfd9ddc26ed7b8112228b920e</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref44"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref44" class="rightTabRefNumLink">44</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit44" data-doi="10.1007/s10008-013-2342-6"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Böckenfeld, N.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Balducci, A.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Determination of Sodium Ion Diffusion Coefficients in Sodium Vanadium Phosphate</span>. <i>J. Solid State Electrochem.</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2014</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>18</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">959</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">964</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1007/s10008-013-2342-6</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref45"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref45" class="rightTabRefNumLink">45</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit45" data-doi="10.1016/j.jpowsour.2014.07.185"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Tillmann, S. D.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Isken, P.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Lex-Balducci, A.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Gel Polymer Electrolyte for Lithium-Ion Batteries Comprising Cyclic Carbonate Moieties</span>. <i>J. Power Sources</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2014</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>271</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">239</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">244</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.jpowsour.2014.07.185</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit45R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">45</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Gel polymer electrolyte for lithium-ion batteries comprising cyclic carbonate moieties</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Tillmann, S. D.; Isken, P.; Lex-Balducci, A.</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Power Sources</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2014</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">271</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue"></span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">239-244</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JPSODZ</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0378-7753</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier B.V.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">A polymer system based on oligo (ethylene glycol) Me ether methacrylate (OEGMA) and cyclic carbonate methacrylate (CCMA) was chosen as matrix to realize high-performance gel polymer electrolytes due to the fact that both monomers are able to interact with the liq. electrolyte, thus, retaining it inside the matrix.  Addnl., OEGMA enables high flexibility, while CCMA provides mech. stability.  The polymer displays a high thermal stability up to 200 °C and a glass transition temp. below room temp. (5 °C) allowing an easy handling of the obtained films.  By immobilizing the liq. electrolyte 1 M LiPF6 in EC:DMC 1:1 w:w in the polymer host a gel polymer electrolyte with a high cond. of 2.3 mS cm-1 at 25 °C and a stable cycling behavior with high capacities and efficiencies in Li(Ni1/3Co1/3Mn1/3)O2 (NCM)/graphite full cells is obtained.  The investigated gel polymer electrolyte is identified as promising electrolyte for lithium-ion batteries, because it combines good electrochem. properties comparable to that of liq. electrolytes with the safety advantage that no leakage of the flammable electrolyte solvents can occur.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGpDMmqJwdtDI7Vg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lh0mkz5VUwB5g"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2cXhtlagsrvF&amp;md5=2a9ab468f9aa45cc4b912c4ad1798249</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref46"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref46" class="rightTabRefNumLink">46</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit46" data-doi="10.1039/c7ta04886f"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Lin, Y.-Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Chen, Y.-M.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Hou, S.-S.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Jan, J.-S.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Lee, Y.-L.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Teng, H.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Diode-Like Gel Polymer Electrolytes for Full-Cell Lithium Ion Batteries</span>. <i>J. Mater. Chem. A</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2017</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>5</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">17476</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">17481</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/c7ta04886f</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit46R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">46</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Diode-like gel polymer electrolytes for full-cell lithium ion batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Lin, Yong-Yi; Chen, Yen-Ming; Hou, Sheng-Shu; Jan, Jeng-Shiung; Lee, Yuh-Lang; Teng, Hsisheng</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Materials Chemistry A: Materials for Energy and Sustainability</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2017</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">5</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">33</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">17476-17481</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JMCAET</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2050-7496</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">This study designs a pos.-intrinsic-neg. (PIN)-diode-like gel polymer electrolyte (GPE) for a full-cell graphite|electrolyte|LiFePO4 Li ion battery to facilitate interfacial ion transfer at both the anode and cathode.  The diode-like GPE comprises an intrinsic poly(acrylonitrile-co-methyl-acrylate)-hosted electrolyte layer, as well as pos. and neg. layers that are synthesized by doping the intrinsic layer with TiO2 and SiO2 nanoparticles, which resp. exhibits pos. and neg. zeta potentials.  The pos. layer that adsorbs PF6- anions is in contact with the LiFePO4 cathode of the battery to facilitate the transfer of Li+ cations across the interface.  The neg. layer, which is in contact with the graphite anode, adsorbs Li+ cations to suppress accumulation and prevent the intercalation of solvated Li+ into the graphitic framework.  The intrinsic layer acts as a neutralization zone to lower the current-rectification effect of the p-n junction.  This PIN-configuration design for electrolytes enhances the ultimate capacity of the full-cell battery, exhibits high rate capacity retention, and increases the lifespan (87% capacity retained after 500 charge-discharge cycles).</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGqG-x_HB9gwfLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lh0mkz5VUwB5g"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2sXht1ektr3L&amp;md5=2e409c98b75b6a0b3e8d64cd3d0c7b0f</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref47"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref47" class="rightTabRefNumLink">47</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit47" data-doi="10.1021/acsami.5b05179"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Di Lecce, D.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Fasciani, C.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Scrosati, B.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Hassoun, J.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">A Gel–Polymer Sn–C/LiMn<sub>0.5</sub>Fe<sub>0.5</sub>PO<sub>4</sub> Battery Using a Fluorine-Free Salt</span>. <i>ACS Appl. Mater. Interfaces</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2015</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>7</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">21198</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">21207</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1021/acsami.5b05179</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit47R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">47</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">A Gel-Polymer Sn-C/LiMn0.5Fe0.5PO4 Battery Using a Fluorine-Free Salt</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Di Lecce, Daniele; Fasciani, Chiara; Scrosati, Bruno; Hassoun, Jusef</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">ACS Applied Materials &amp; Interfaces</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2015</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">7</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">38</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">21198-21207</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">AAMICK</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1944-8244</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">American Chemical Society</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Safety and environmental issues, because of the contemporary use of common liq. electrolytes, fluorinated salts, and LiCoO2-based cathodes in com. Li-ion batteries, might be efficiently mitigated by employing alternative gel-polymer battery configurations and new electrode materials.  Herein we study a lithium-ion polymer cell formed by combining a LiMn0.5Fe0.5PO4 olivine cathode, prepd. by simple solvothermal pathway, a nanostructured Sn-C anode, and a LiBOB-contg. PVdF-based gel electrolyte.  The polymer electrolyte, here analyzed in terms of electrochem. stability by impedance spectroscopy (EIS) and voltammetry, reveals full compatibility for cell application.  The LiBOB electrolyte salt and the electrochem. delithiaded Mn0.5Fe0.5PO4 have a higher thermal stability compared to conventional LiPF6 and Li0.5CoO2, as confirmed by thermogravimetric anal. (TGA) and by galvanostatic cycling at high temp.  LiMn0.5Fe0.5PO4 and Sn-C, showing in lithium half-cell a capacity of about 120 and 350 mAh g-1, resp., within the gelled electrolyte configuration are combined in a full Li-ion polymer battery delivering a stable capacity of about 110 mAh g-1, with working voltage ranging from 2.8 to 3.6 V.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGrU4P4U94z9gbVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lh0mkz5VUwB5g"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXhsVKls7zO&amp;md5=837ed24696c7b91b8081a1df7f8a37c7</span></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i13">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge on the <a href="/" class="ext-link">ACS Publications website</a> at DOI: <a href="/doi/abs/10.1021/acsami.8b02768" class="ext-link">10.1021/acsami.8b02768</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">Characterization for the P(VDF-HFP) GPE;         <script nonce="90da8f66dc46b325-SJC">
(function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	}); 

	$('.share_button').on('click', function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	$("#pane-m1con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Figures'});
	});

	$("#pane-m2con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'References'});
	});

	$("#pane-m3con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Supporting Info'});
	});

	$('.tab__close').on('click', function(){
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Close'});
	}); 



})();

</script>

<script nonce="90da8f66dc46b325-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="90da8f66dc46b325-SJC">
"use strict"

	/* 
	Create an in-page pop-up message, only for the InfoCentral homepage, that will gather email registrants for the library marketing list.
	 
	Needs the end point
	*/

var infoCentralCapture = (function() {

    //Detect mobile device
    window.mobilecheck = function() {
        var check = false;
        (function(a){if(/(android|bb\d+|meego).+mobile|avantgo|bada\/|blackberry|blazer|compal|elaine|fennec|hiptop|iemobile|ip(hone|od)|iris|kindle|lge |maemo|midp|mmp|mobile.+firefox|netfront|opera u|g560|gene|gf\-5|g\-mo|go(\.w|od)|gr(ad|un)|haie|hcit|hd\-(m|p|t)|hei\-|hi(pt|ta)|hp( i|ip)|hs\-c|ht(c(\-| |_|a|g|p|s|t)|tp)|hu(aw|tc)|i\-(20|go|ma)|i230|iac( |\-|\/)|ibro|idea|ig01|ikom|im1k|inno|ipaq|iris|ja(t|v)a|jbro|jemu|jigs|kddi|keji|kgt( |\/)|klon|kpt |kwc\-|kyo(c|k)|le(no|xi)|lg( g|\/(k|l|u)|50|54|\-[a-w])|libw|lynx|m1\-w|m3ga|m50\/|ma(te|ui|xo)|mc(01|21|ca)|m\-cr|me(rc|ri)|mi(o8|oa|ts)|mmef|mo(01|02|bi|de|do|t(\-| |o|v)|zz)|mt(50|p1|v )|mwbp|mywa|n10[0-2]|n20[2-3]|n30(0|2)|n50(0|2|5)|n7(0(0|1)|10)|ne((c|m)\-|on|tf|wf|wg|wt)|nok(6|i)|nzph|o2im|op(ti|wv)|oran|owg1|p800|pan(a|d|t)|pdxg|pg(13|\-([1-8]|c))|phil|pire|pl(ay|uc)|pn\-2|po(ck|rt|se)|prox|psio|pt\-g|qa\-a|qc(07|12|21|32|60|\-[2-7]|i\-)|qtek|r380|r600|raks|rim9|ro(ve|zo)|s55\/|sa(ge|ma|mm|ms|ny|va)|sc(01|h\-|oo|p\-)|sdk\/|se(c(\-|0|1)|47|mc|nd|ri)|sgh\-|shar|sie(\-|m)|sk\-0|sl(45|id)|sm(al|ar|b3|it|t5)|so(ft|ny)|sp(01|h\-|v\-|v )|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(a.substr(0,4))) check = true;})(navigator.userAgent||navigator.vendor||window.opera);
              return check;
        };

    var _isMobile = window.mobilecheck();
    if (_isMobile) {
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').addClass('mobile');
    }

    var emailValid = "",
        time = 3000,
        btnStatus = true,
        errorStatus = false,
        errormessage = "<p class='gdpr_err'><b>Please Enter a valid email address<b><p>";

    function init() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
            if (cookieExist) {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
                return false;
            } else {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
                gdprMessage();
            }
            //Events
            $('#closebtn').on("click", hideForm);

            //Handle submit
            $('#gdpr-message-btn').on("click", function(event) {
                handleClick();
            });

            // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
            // $(document).click(function(event) {
            // 	event.stopPropagation();
            //   console.log(event.target);
            //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
            //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
            //     $(this).off();
            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag('event', 'GDPR Modal', { 'event_category': 'Pubs GDPR', 'event_label':'GDPR Dismissal'});
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>


                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="90da8f66dc46b325-SJC">
var currentJournal = "ACS Applied Materials &amp;amp; Interfaces";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>
